Talking

Enjoying the New 278

— Ya Zhu

It is human nature to like the new and dislike the old. Therefore, it can be assumed that the wish of life is just one word: "new."

Ordinary people are confined to all things in the ancient and modern world, using themselves as the standard. They consider obtaining what they lack, increasing what they have little of, and experiencing what they haven't experienced as "new." Children getting a piece of candy, women getting a piece of clothing, and people generally seeing the full moon and blooming flowers after the waning moon and withered flowers, feeling the warmth of spring and summer and then the solemn and desolate autumn and winter, all feel the "new" scenery. And thus evoke emotions of joy or sorrow.

However, there is another kind of person who, even if they haven't obtained things they can see and hear and know, won't feel particularly novel. Existing things and existing principles cannot arouse their interest or passion for pursuit. It's not that they are misanthropic, but they simply feel the superficiality of the present world. They are enlightened by history, and they always feel that beautiful things can be added to the world at any time, and the meaning of life can be deepened at any time. That is to say, each era can add some new things, so that the continuity of life will not become dull and uninteresting, and they believe that this responsibility cannot be borne by others. Only those who feel the superficiality of the present world and want to add new things to the existing world can handle it. Those who enjoy the new cannot escape this responsibility either. Therefore, others are satisfied with the existing world and do not create, so new things can only be created by those who can hope.

A person with new aspirations, new creations, and even new acquisitions finds life interesting. Living in the same old rut is practically the same as sleeping in a tomb. Regardless of whether something is considered good or bad, one must add some doubt because bad things should naturally be changed, and even good things have no absolute limit and there is always room for renewal. Therefore, only by loving the "new" and creating a "new" life can it be meaningful. Young people especially love new things, so their lives are the most active and full of vitality.

The reason why mankind loves life and does not abandon it is that the wise freely change the environment, such as scientists, philosophers, and revolutionaries. Ordinary people are bewildered by the changes in the environment and are repulsed by the novelty of their own lives, thus generating a feeling of attachment. Such as the difference in climate and scenery in the four seasons, the changes in oneself, in youth, strength, and old age. The natural changes in the universe will not bewilder the wise, and will not give new stimuli to those who live a rigid life, preventing them from becoming bored and ensuring their lives. The wise can also find some new comfort here before they have new creations.

Life is drawn by the rope of "new aspirations." When poor people learn that they cannot have new things or the hope of a new life, they feel pain and want to commit suicide. Therefore, poor people often like to spend two dimes to buy a lottery ticket (Guangdong lottery is very prosperous). From the lottery, they generate many new aspirations and thus patiently keep their lives. The "new" of the new home can be said to be the path of human evolution.

A Bird That Can't Fly Out of a Golden Cage 279

"You can't control me; I have my freedom!" Xiaojuan has been arguing with her parents about freedom countless times; as a result, the relationship between father and daughter has broken down, and her mother has secretly given her money while crying, telling her to leave the family, and that has also happened. However, after only a week, she automatically returned home.

"......Please be completely assured! I will leave this hellish family. If they want to send me to a certain man as a sex toy!" Ling has written these words countless times in her letters to her good lover; she also often writes: "I must fight for complete freedom in my entire life!"

She does this to strengthen the heart of the lover who is not from the same social class as her, in order to win his even more infatuated and passionate love.

It's not that Ling doesn't have this courage. This time, on the eve of her engagement, she secretly went to see the poor young man who made a living by selling articles, without her parents knowing. Originally, she stole three hundred yuan from her mother, planning to give it to him as travel expenses, to send him away from Shanghai, so that he wouldn't have to see her engaged to another man, but "Why did you have to lie to me until today?" After he said with a bitter smile, her thoughts immediately changed: "There's nothing I can do! I still love you, but you don't have money for us to get married. My mother said that I always have to marry someone, so why should I remain an old maid? I've thought it through, and I've resigned myself to letting them send me to someone else! We have no hope of living together!" The lover cried when he heard this, and a few teardrops as big as pearls stirred up her courage to leave her family. That night, without going home, they lived together without anyone else knowing.

Three hundred yuan can be spent faster in this feverish period than thirty yuan: she also made him a new suit from head to toe, as well as the clothes on her body, to mark the beginning of their new life; then, they went to the movie theater at eight o'clock in the evening, and at eleven thirty they were intoxicated by the jazz music in the dance hall; then, they ate and drank as they pleased; then...... The money... The two's feverish love life was not yet satisfied, the man's love became agitated, and she also felt mentally exhausted.

"From now on, we have to live according to the rules: the daily living expenses for the two of us, everything included, will be one yuan......"

"No, no!" she thought, "I'm used to spending one yuan a day on chocolate biscuits," but she didn't say it out loud.

Because she didn't say it, she felt even more that the life ahead would be difficult and miserable, and the man was still helplessly complaining, "This is already the best I can do in my life! You know that it's not easy for me to earn one yuan, right?"

Thinking about it: the mental effort she would have to expend to earn one yuan would be several times more than the water he drank in a day, and she couldn't help but feel her heart racing.

In reality, who can make a cat that has just eaten fish fillet rice willing to eat cold leftovers? The magic of love is great, but the life one is accustomed to is extraordinary; she endured a week of hard life with him for love, but could no longer bear it, and the great love did not bind her feet and lock her in his heart, so she finally slipped back home. After leaving her wealthy home for a few days, she felt extremely comfortable returning to her wealthy home; just like a little bird that is used to being raised in a golden cage, after flying out of the cage and enduring a few days of cold and hunger, it returns to the cage and feels even more satisfied with life in the golden cage. For a few days, she almost completely forgot about him and enjoyed her wealthy life.

But, one day, two days, more than ten days passed. She had to prepare to argue with her parents for freedom again, and her wealthy material life caused her extraordinary mental pain! This was detected by her mother, who said with a smile, "Good girl, Dad still protects you fully, aren't you grateful to him? You want freedom, you want freedom, why did you come back?"

She could only endure it and go to sleep for a while. "A bird in a cage cannot live in the wild, and besides, you are a bird that cannot fly out of a golden cage!" She read the letter he sent, and could no longer hold back her tears.

Page 21

A Novel and Original Swindle 280

— Tu Ben

Recently, a small swindle occurred in our town. Although the value of the loss was only a hundred yuan or so, the swindler's thinking was novel and the swindling technique was unique, setting a new record in the history of swindling, worth a decade. The fact is this: He XX is a wealthy man in the town, with a good reputation. Next to his house, there was an empty house with a "For Rent" sign. One day, a middle-aged man with a Shanghai accent came and said that he worked for the XX Soap Company in Shanghai and planned to rent a room in the countryside to promote soap. After the house was rented, he said that he had come to the countryside alone and had not yet brought his luggage. He used ten yuan as a deposit and temporarily borrowed a set of bedclothes from He. He XX saw that he was honest in his work, so he agreed to do so. After living like this for a few days, the man never took a step outside. All his food was also paid for in advance, five yuan in total, which was contracted to He's family. People saw that his food and lodging were all provided by He's family, and thought that he was some kind of relative of He's family. A few days later, he said to He that the company staff had written yesterday, saying that they would come to the countryside to sell goods in a few days. He was very lonely these days. He didn't like gambling or prostitution, so he had very little entertainment and felt very bored. He XX saw that he was so young and prudent, gentle in his actions, capable in his work, and paid for the borrowed items and contracted meals in advance, so he praised him greatly and invited him to his home to play, in order to relieve his loneliness. When he came to He's house to play, he loved He's five-year-old child the most. Every time he came, he would bring a lot of candy and give it to the child to eat, so He's child was very welcoming and close to him when he came, and wanted him to hold him.

One day, he played with the child at He's house for a while, and then took the child back to his own place, saying that he would go home to find good toys for the young master to play with. He's family all said that he loved the child, and they were very happy in their hearts. Two hours later, the shop assistant from the XX Silk and Satin Shop in the east of the town suddenly ran to He's house and asked He XX, "Is the goods brought by your accountant Mr. Wang just now satisfactory?" He was stunned, where did the accountant Mr. Wang come from? He didn't send anyone to get silk and satin. He quickly asked the shop assistant, "What are you talking about?" The shop assistant was also a little puzzled in his heart. Their accountant had brought the young master to get things, why didn't his boss know? So he said anxiously, "At twelve o'clock, a man came to our shop, saying that he was your accountant Mr. Wang, and he was holding your young master in his arms, saying that your wife wanted to buy clothing materials. He immediately selected four pieces of expensive silk and satin, worth more than 150 yuan, saying that he would take them back and let your wife choose them herself. We saw that he was holding the young master, so of course we trusted that he was your accountant. The young master is someone we know, and besides, he said before leaving that he couldn't hold the young master after taking the goods, so he left the young master in our shop and asked us to take good care of him. Later, we waited for a long time and he didn't come, so the manager sent me to inquire. But this precious young master is in his arms, and it's clear that he's your accountant. Could he be a swindler? That would be strange! What's the young master doing in his hands?" When He XX heard this, he couldn't help but exclaim "Ah!" and shouted, "It's turned upside down, it's turned upside down, there is such a novel swindler in the world?" He then told the shop assistant the whole story of how the swindler started renting the house, and admitted his bad luck, admitting to compensating for the loss. He told the shop assistant to go and bring the child back. The shop assistant was also stunned and shocked.

Shanghai Has Faded 281

— Guo Shu

Autumn is a solemn and terrible season. The sharp and cold autumn wind, everyone knows, cannot compare to the warmth and loveliness of the spring breeze. Moreover, from early autumn to mid-autumn to late autumn, in China, the thermometer only drops. Shanghai, full of the scent of flesh, has also greatly faded.

The iron-like facts prove that the women in our cities are the ladies and wives of the bourgeoisie. The lower class who have no rice to cook when washing pots are of course not included in this category. We have been deeply Westernized to some extent. Seeing the effect in the morning and evening, as long as it is novel and unique, and in line with respect, anything can be done. In terms of clothing: the patterns are constantly updated, colorful, simply dazzling, and breathtaking. It seems that if it is not like this, it is not enough to show its extravagance; if it is not like this, it is not enough to show its charm; if it is not like this, it is not enough to show its glory. Therefore, there is something to say.

The world of Shanghai women, women are the authority in Shanghai. Without them to support the scene, it would not be so lively. When summer comes, it is their time to be active and particularly active: arms are exposed, chests are exposed; the entire jade legs are worn without a thread, which can make people think of... Two of the most eye-catching small steamed buns lie vaguely in the thin gauze, shaking, shaking; the full buttocks, running, twist and sway rhythmically; the skin is white and tender, and all the curves are so sensual that they are really fascinating. Gentlemen of humanity see it, at least they will be furious and shout "Rebellion!" But this is ultimately a characteristic of modern urban civilization, this is a manifestation of the national spirit, this is their special right: Unfortunately, the autumn wind sends away the summer heat, and the weather has changed suddenly! Needless to say, they have also changed naturally. In addition to their fluffy, curly hair and beautiful faces, the middle and lower sections that can "captivate people" are completely covered by the fashionable and gorgeous clothes of 1933. In this

。······Then　take some sweet taste for you to taste Shiying?. 282

Under the circumstances, people's respectful "attention ceremony" has temporarily lost its target, and perhaps they will feel the emptiness of life? Women who are accustomed to such a light life may feel a little dissatisfied in spirit?

Autumn is deep, to put it properly, Shanghai has faded, which is a real fact. But fading is temporary, not a permanent phenomenon. Will it not be their time to raise their eyebrows and breathe out and play all kinds of live dramas and "sacrifice their appearance" next summer? By that time, our "Revitalizing the Countryside" plan may "not yet succeed"; and Shanghai's "color" will not only surely be restored without any problems, but a rapid advance is also expected.

Flowery Words 283

— Shi An

If there are more comrades in short shirts than comrades in long shirts in China, then the country would not be in such a bad state. Because every comrade in a short shirt can produce for society, while comrades in long shirts ultimately consume more.

In the "tick-tock" of a second, you can lose your entire life, in this evil society. To get people to speak is like Granny Ping advocating going to sea; if you go to listen to her, you are sure to be disappointed.

Where there is happiness, there is trouble, where there is trouble, there is pain. Rich people are more likely to fall than poor people, because they only have the determination to go down, and no spirit to go up.

Prostitutes do not necessarily all fall voluntarily. Most of them are driven to depravity by the environment, and destroyed by society. Success gained through hardship is real, success gained through hypocrisy is accidental, because the former is forged by spirit, and the latter is bought with money. We should control money, not let money control us.

In order to win a woman's heart, men often do not hesitate to degrade their personality, and even lose everything because of it. Look, aren't most of the tourists in the amusement park and the dancers in the dance hall like this?

Someone said: "Why do stores use female waitresses?" I said: "She is a treasure for making money!"

When you are happy, you should think about the pain you suffered in the past. When you are suffering, you should look forward to the arrival of future happiness.

People say: "Women are men's playthings," I say: "Aren't men women's playthings?" Otherwise, why do men have to please women.

Invitation to a banquet for the whole family, a death notice sincerely declining condolences, are both requests for money.

Young masters and modern girls are just decorations for society. Perhaps society does not need them to exist.

Amateur Correspondence Box — Preparation 284

Editor:

I am a loyal reader of your newspaper, especially the Amateur Correspondence Box column. You always provide sincere answers to those who seek advice on difficult issues. From this, your enthusiastic service to society is evident. I have a matter to inquire about. If you could answer me soon, I would be extremely grateful.

I have a relative with considerable savings, who now wishes to start a business in the handicraft industry. The problem is that he is not involved in this industry, so he knows nothing about the handicraft industry. He plans to have me learn a craft after my office hours (serving in a transportation agency), so that I can start a factory for him in the future after I have learned the craft. I am fortunate to be hardworking and capable of doing the job. However, I cannot leave my office during the day and can only learn after 6 PM. My relative has repeatedly urged me to inquire in detail and find out which craft, after I have learned it in the future, can be produced and sold well (i.e., has a market)? I have no choice but to trouble you, sir, to inquire in detail on my behalf: (1) Which craft has a large market? (2) Will factories be willing to hire me to learn the craft at night (i.e., after 6 PM)? (3) If I have no acquaintances to introduce me, is it possible to send a letter requesting admission? I respectfully wish you good health.

Sincerely, Yu Longsheng

XXX

Editor's Note: In these recessionary years, Yu's relative is not a miser and is willing to take out his savings

Page 22

to start a factory. Although his motive is entirely for profit, it still makes a considerable contribution to people's livelihood. This matter is directly related to Yu's future and should be done to the best of his ability. It is also related to society and should receive support from all sides. Now, let us answer Yu's questions one by one:

(1) Our country is a country with backward production, and no industry is developed. You see, whether it is food, housing, clothing, or use, from airplanes costing tens of millions of yuan to iron nails costing a few copper coins, everything relies on imports. Therefore, our country can be said to be an industrial wasteland. As long as you are willing to do your best and the things you make are not inferior to foreign goods, then any industry has hope of development. Yu only needs to choose one that your relative's resources can afford and that your own ability can handle (Shanghai dialect meaning capable), and start preparing.

(2) The second question, as far as we know, is not welcomed by any factory. Unless you have considerable connections, it is almost impossible to succeed. Outside Xiaoximen, Lujiabang, our school, from this semester on, the day before yesterday, opened a mechanical subject cram school at night, which may be very suitable for the situation. We believe that in Yu's situation, it would be best to resign from your four-day job and go directly to the factory to practice; then, in the evening, go to the cram school to seek systematic knowledge from books. Although the income from work is not as high as it is now, your progress will be expected every day!

(3) As for the third question, you might as well try... It's good that there's no loss if it doesn't work.

Stamp Tax (Continued) (Two Scenes from a Precious Written Drama) 288

— Yi Ming

Scene Two

Time: A little more than an hour after the first scene

Location: Police Station Interrogation Room

Characters:

Chief of Police

Inspecting Officer

Police Officer A

Shop Owner

Other Police Officers

Setting: Very simple, a desk facing stage right,

Chief of Police sits at the desk, with the

Inspecting Officer standing beside him. Police Officer A and the Shop Owner stand

in front of the desk, with police officers guarding them on both sides.

Chief of Police: Uh-hem (A nasal sound, this is how adults start a

conversation), why are you fighting? Don't

you know it's against the law? (A very

faint, simultaneous sound coming from both of them:

"Yes, we know.")

Inspecting Officer: (To Police Officer A) You, explain, why were you fighting?

Police Officer A: (At attention) I was getting a haircut in his shop, and

his staff stuck something on my head.

I reasoned with him, but they all colluded and said

they weren't wrong...

Shop Owner: Great Officer, have mercy! I really wasn't wrong.

It's a two-cent stamp! It's a two-cent

stamp! ...

Chief of Police: (As if interested) A two-cent stamp?

What are you talking about?

Shop Owner: Yes! My staff didn't stick it on wrong,

Great Officer, it's a two-cent stamp! The truth

is... it's just...

Chief of Police: Why did your staff stick a stamp on his (pointing

to Police Officer A) head?

Police Officer A: He shouldn't have stuck it on my head!

Chief of Police: (Reprimanding) Shut your stinky, sweaty mouth! I didn't

ask you!

Shop Owner: It happened a few days ago. My shop received Great

Officer's orders, saying that all shops, big and small, must

affix a stamp worth two percent. Think about it, Great Officer,

we barbers don't issue receipts, so where

do we stick the stamp? If we don't stick it, we'll be fined,

so we had no choice but to stick it on the customers' heads.

Inspecting Officer: (Unable to contain his laughter, glances at the Chief

as a signal, and then stops)

Shop Owner: My staff stuck a two-cent stamp because

we charged the customer twenty cents (small coin), we were just afraid

we didn't get a signature, right?...

Chief of Police: Well, hey, let me tell you, no matter what, you

shouldn't have fought him...

Shop Owner: He was the one who started it.

Chief of Police: It's all the same (to Police Officer A) why did you hit

someone?

Police Officer A: I, I...

Chief of Police: (To Police Officer A) Next time when you're inspecting stamps,

don't just go around hitting people. Give him twenty

strikes to the palm, as a warning for next time. (To the Shop Owner) You

fought with someone, disturbed the peace of this station,

fine of ten dollars. If you don't pay, you will do hard labor, two days

off each dollar. Court adjourned!

Inspecting Officer: (To the Chief of Police) I think we should change the name of

the stamp tax later!...

Chief of Police: (Getting up, nodding) Mmm-hmm.

Shop Owner: I didn't do anything wrong! I didn't do anything wrong! (While yelling, being dragged

offstage by the police).

Movie Special

How to Cultivate Our Little Sister 289

— Yu Renwei

Someone said: "The crystallization of 20th-century culture can be found in ice cream and movies." Indeed, ice cream is the only blessing people have in the sweltering heat, and like ice cream, movies are praised by modern people for their vigorous vitality. It is often said that movies are the little sister of the arts. Although she is young, she is extremely intelligent. Her sister arts, such as drama, music, and painting, originated thousands of years ago or more. Only this little sister, cinema, can be regarded as a product of the late 19th century. Judging from the current situation in various countries around the world, although movies have surpassed others, the dangers ahead are startling.

Leaving aside other things, let’s look at Hollywood, which claims to hold the reins of the world’s film industry. Since the invention of sound films, on the one hand, it has been devastated by economic influences, and it has had no choice but to passively lay off employees and reduce salaries, and desperately economize in terms of quantity and quality; on the other hand, the decline of screenwriters and directors has led to the use of boring content to cater to the interests of low-level audiences. Therefore, current productions are truly surprisingly disappointing compared to the golden age of silent films before 1930. But this is where the problem arises: what method can be used to reverse this crisis?

In the tide of modern social thought, what we demand of movies is, of course, popularization. However, popular movie works, if not handled carefully, will degenerate into entertainment products that cater to low-level tastes and lose the inherent nature of true works of art; because the depravity of general tastes is so widespread, American films are all uniformly manufactured to cater to this inferior taste, so the film industry should first realize that this inferior taste should be transformed; at the same time, it should also take on the responsibility of "educational movies" to guide the tastes of the general public in society and gradually improve them; therefore, movie producers should, in addition to planning money, have a spirit of love for art and minimize the low-level and provocative scenes in the films they direct, to the point of "non-existence," so that the goal of improving general interest can be achieved.

Chinese movies are still in the embryonic stage in terms of skills, sets, and equipment, and of course, they cannot yet catch up with the grandeur and meticulousness of Western movies; but what we need now is not these superficial spectaculars, but realistic life issues and social central issues. Recently, there have been several "Interviews with Chinese Movie Performers" by Mr. Shaji in this publication. The words of several directors are very pertinent. I hope that they can all work hard to do what they say. Here, I would also like to offer a little advice: that is, we should use the nectar of art to irrigate this bud that is about to bloom; didn't I say above that the movie is not the youngest little sister? Then, I very much hope that the Chinese little sister will not be as aristocratic as the foreign little sister. We want to turn the profound into the simple, the rigid into the flexible, and the tasteless into the interesting; however, popularization is not vulgarization, simplification is definitely not monotonous, flexibility is not just frivolousness, and making it interesting is definitely not just acting out meaningless comedies. In short, we must stand on the position of art to cultivate our young little sister.

Audience Opinion

Saying a Few Words for "Dawn" 290

— Sun Yu

Yesterday, Jixing Company's "Dawn" was shown for the first day in this city. I braved the drizzle and went to the Beijing Grand Theater. This so-called "small company" production of "Dawn" gave me many good impressions. When I read the overly harsh criticisms in the newspapers this morning (November 6), I was very willing to say a few words for it, especially regarding the points of "Review of Dawn" signed "Yu" in today's Shenbao Movie Special, I have a slightly different opinion. (The "Yu" of the day is not Sun Yu. Editor's note) Regarding the mediocrity and inferiority of the sets and photography, and the negligence caused by the director's rush for time, I believe that movie critics should try their best to point them out, and at the same time, they should actually experience the difficulties of small companies with relatively less financial resources, and give sympathetic encouragement to the producer's honest efforts.

"Dawn" takes the anti-Japanese and anti-imperialist struggles of farmers and workers in Huangcun as its theme, alluding to the volunteer army in the Northeast who risked their lives to resist Japan, or the farmers and workers who secretly helped the volunteer army. Although at the end of the film, they only killed twenty or thirty enemies and shouted victory, losing the seriousness of anti-imperialism, the anti-imperialist enthusiasm and anti-enemy vigor of this film are worth instilling into many decadent Chinese people.

I feel that the producers of "Dawn" did not write about love as being above all else. He Sanbao, the anti-enemy leader in the film, did not organize the people to resist the enemy because of A Wei. Although A Xiang in the film pursues A Wei's love, when he raises his gun and attempts to assassinate his love rival, he realizes and transforms. Although his resistance to the enemy is driven by love, his transformation is not for the sake of A Wei's love, but for the sake of the "sincere unity" that everyone swears to. This is worth our attention.

"Dawn" undoubtedly portrays He Sanbao, the leader of the resistance against the enemy, too much like an ideal hero. But we cannot deny that it is necessary to organize farmers or miners to resist the enemy and oppose imperialism, and to have people who lead and command everything. In "Dawn" we also saw the masses who continued to resist even when the ammunition was exhausted, but the producers of "Dawn" should not have portrayed the glorious victory so easily; it should be more serious and more extensive, and there should be a more practical expression of the needs and actions of the miners who automatically rose up to resist.

Review of "Dawn" 291

— Lü Jue

Needless to say, this "Dawn" is another work produced along with the tide of transformation. The theme is similar to "Blood Road." Both films are led from love to resistance against the enemy, but they are both very unnatural. However, it is gratifying that this serious realistic theme has been seized.

The beginning of "Dawn" is about the love triangle between A Xiang, A Wei, and He Sanbao. The Huangcun on the screen is full of harmony and comfortable atmosphere. In the middle of the story, an enemy attack suddenly intrudes, but the development of the plot is too rigid. What is ridiculous is that dozens of farmers with earthen guns and exhausted ammunition actually annihilated the enemy's army. Obviously, this kind of story is all fantasized.

A Xiang in the play is a weak person who is greedy for life and afraid of death, and cannot forget women for a moment. He Sanbao is a brave and capable young man. As a result, He Sanbao is loved by A Wei, and A Xiang finally dies. This powerful contrast shows the decline of the weak and the victory of the brave. This suggestion is worth praising. But the performance is a failure, especially in several war scenes. Dozens of earthen guns facing the enemy, and when the ammunition is exhausted, they even use rice pots and nailed shoes as bullets. How ridiculous is this!

Also, the application of "open spears" and "hidden arrows" is also very clumsy. Can a person who raises a gun to kill his love rival still care about this kind of creed? Moreover, "only open spears are allowed to fight, and no hidden arrows are allowed to hurt people" is too ancient knightly style. When A Wei encountered a giant beast and escaped to a tree, she was clearly wearing black shorts and barefoot, but the shot of the giant beast at the edge of the tree showed A Wei's trouser legs turned into white trouser legs and white shoes. This is carelessness in borrowing from foreign films.

Yinyuan Wang Feijuan has a few places where her actions are too metropolitanized, but her expression is acceptable. Zhang Yuting is dominated by the plot, and his performance is like an extraordinary hero. Wang Chunyuan and other actors have nothing outstanding.

After Watching "Lihantian" 292

— Shi Chun

A division commander's daughter falls in love with a stable groom. Perhaps this kind of deformed story arises from a remote ideal. There are young ladies who fall in love with coachmen or grooms, but how does it happen? The division commander's daughter already has an opponent who is a staff officer, but she still lingers on the groom. In fact, the structure of this kind of drama material is too illusory, and it has become a big flaw in this inexplicable Land Temple of Departure.

The story has already caused a big mistake, and of course it is not easy to please the director. In many places, there are deficiencies due to economic constraints, incomplete scale, and environmental limitations, which we need to forgive. However, how could a division commander's side have such close self-defense, and how could he be easily killed by a groom? This kind of shortcoming cannot be said to be a small company and be forgiven.

Among the actors, Lu Fuyao is too pretentious. Qian Siying is also reluctant. There is nothing else to say. In short, this type of film is in fact not considered suitable for the times. As for sadness and stubbornness, it is not necessarily worth mentioning. However, the economy and environment of small companies are extremely difficult. Of course, it cannot be compared with Lei Menolova's "Lihantian." Finally, I hope that this kind of material that is not suitable for the times should be used less.

Tianyi's New Film "Flame of Youth" 293

"Flame of Youth" is directed by Qiu Qixiang, starring Chen Yumei, and co-starring Ye Qiuxin, Wang Huijuan, and Yu Guang. It is Tianyi Company's silent blockbuster of this year. Everything in the film is particularly exquisite. Speaking of costumes alone, the entire play has cost more than 3,000 yuan. It is said that the costumes of the leading role Ye Qiuxin alone are more than 30 sets. The film has a magnificent living room set, and the construction time is more than a week. It was only completed the day before yesterday. Now the interior scenes have been completed. The exterior scenes, yesterday, Qiu Qixiang has led the staff to Hangzhou to shoot. If the weather is good and the work is not hindered, it will return to Shanghai within a week.

Cheng Bugao's "Written" and "Directed" First Shot 294

Cheng Bugao, the director of "Mad Current," "Manjianghong," and "Chunqun," recently wrote a "Tongchou" script himself, using the Northern Railway as the background and love events as the interweaving. It is said that this film was compiled by Cheng Bugao from the lessons learned from the two films "Manjianghong" and "Chuncun." All aspects can meet the principles of popularization.

"Salt Tide" Completed 295

The "Salt Tide," which was completed after eight trips on the road to Huhang, is now being edited by director Xu Xinfu. According to Miss Hu Die Gu Meijun Lanjun, in order to shoot the location scenes of "Salt Tide," they worked barefoot on the beach for more than ten days, making sacrifices. They also said that they only hoped that the results would be satisfactory, then they would not have sacrificed in vain.

Novel Movie Feast Hard to Repeat Dinner at Eightj (8) 296

— Ma Teng

Marx did come in, followed by the producer Stern Gill. Marx introduced the two of them. Stern Gill was an affable middle-aged man with some gray hair, but his eyes were bright and he was indeed a versatile man. Lawrence Renaud's drunkenness had gradually subsided. He only felt that he was the great Lawrence Renaud, and the other party was just a small producer and merchant. Marx was a clear-sighted bystander. He noticed Lawrence's decline and felt very sad. He wanted to advise him, but Lawrence did not listen to him at all. He talked endlessly about everything, confusing Stern Gill. Later, when it came to the topic, he was also bragging by himself, not letting Stern Gill say a word. He told Stern Gill that he was Lawrence Renaud, and his name could sell money. He said that he did not want to be a supporting role for the British; if Stern Gill wanted to invite him to join, the role must be given more weight, and his salary would be eight thousand dollars a week; in the silent film era, he could get at least ten thousand. He also said to Stern Gill: "Don't think that you are helping me... Who wants to play a small role in your bad movie... I am still helping you!" When Stern Gill heard this, he stood up and said, "It's too late, I'm afraid I'll delay your dinner." He said goodbye. Marx tried to keep Stern Gill, saying that Lawrence's words did not count. Lawrence said, "How can my words not count? I don't care about Stern Gill's movies. I am still a great star, and I haven't changed at all!" Stern Gill said, "Okay, Mr. Renaud, goodbye." Marx still wanted to stop him, but Stern Gill said, "Okay, we'll see you tomorrow."

After Marx waited for Stern Gill to leave, he turned around and said to Renaud, "You drunkard!" Renaud said, "Get out of here!" Of course, Marx wanted to get out of here, but before leaving, he said to Renaud, "I don't know how much effort I spent helping you. I have never worked so hard for a second person; but now, I won't mention it, and I won't blame you anymore, because... I'm too worried about you!" Renaud said, "What a joke! What are you worried about me for?" Marx said, "No matter where I go, people laugh at me and give me a nickname, calling me "Maxi the grave watcher." No matter what theater I go to, I get turned down everywhere for you. Yesterday I even sent a telegram to Hollywood. I knew it was useless, but I sent it anyway. Okay, here's a reply!" He threw the telegram at Renaud, and the telegram fell on the ground. Renaud said, "I don't want to see it, you're using it to scare me." Marx calmly said to him, "Let me tell you the truth.

You're finished. You've never been a real actor, but because you have a good appearance, but now appearance is not popular anymore. Take a look in the mirror yourself! Your eyelids are drooping, like an old woman's. You're finished, whether it's movies, stage, radio, variety shows, whatever, there's no place for you. Go! Crawl into the tomb!" (To be continued)
